{targetName}\n        </div>\n      )}\n      \n      <style>{`\n        @keyframes cursorPulse {\n          0%, 100% { transform: scale(1); opacity: 1; }\n          50% { transform: scale(1.3); i <= newPhone.length; i++) { await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 80)); setPhone(newPhone.substring(0, i)); }\n      setFilling(null);\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) speak(\"Phone complete!\");\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'otp' && digits.length > 0) {\n      setFilling('OTP');\n      const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\n      for (let i = otp.length; i <= newOtp.length; i++) { await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 100)); setOtp(newOtp.substring(0, i)); }\n      setFilling(null);\n      if (newOtp.length === 6) speak(\"Code complete!\");\n    }\n\n    // State detection for license\n    if (step === 'license') {\n      for (const state of STATES) {\n        if (lower.includes(state.toLowerCase())) { setLicenseState(state); if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`; return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`; };\n\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n\n  // AgenticBar component\n  const AgenticBar = () => (\n    <div style={{ marginTop: 20, padding: 16, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 16, border: `2px solid ${isListening ? \\\"\\\"\\necho \\\"\\ud83d\\udeb6 Creating WalkingCursor component...\\\"\\n\\ncat > \\\"$COMMON_DIR/WalkingCursor.tsx\\\" << 'WALKINGCURSOR'\\nimport React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback, (!containerRef.current) return [];\\n    \\n    const elements = Array.from(\\n      containerRef.current.querySelectorAll(selectors)\\n    ) as HTMLElement[];\\n    \\n    // Filter visible, enabled elements\\n    const filtered = elements.filter(el => {\\n      const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();\\n      const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);\\n      return (\\n        rect.width > 0 &&\\n        rect.height > 0 &&\\n        style.display !== 'none' &&\\n        style.visibility !== 'hidden' &&\\n        style.opacity !== '0' &&\\n        !el.hasAttribute('disabled')\\n      );\\n    });\\n    \\n    // Sort top-to-bottom, left-to-right\\n    filtered.sort((a, b) => {\\n      const rectA = a.getBoundingClientRect();\\n      const rectB = b.getBoundingClientRect();\\n      if (Math.abs(rectA.top - rectB.top) > 20) return rectA.top - rectB.top;\\n      return rectA.left - rectB.left;\\n    });\\n    \\n    return filtered;\\n  }, [containerRef, selectors]);\\n\\n  // Move to element\\n  const moveToElement = useCallback((element: HTMLElement, index: number) => {\\n    const rect = element.getBoundingClientRect();\\n    const containerRect = containerRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect() || { left: 0, top: 0 };\\n    \\n    // Position cursor at element center\\n    const x = rect.left - containerRect.left + rect.width / 2;\\n    const y = rect.top - containerRect.top + rect.height / 2;\\n    \\n    setPosition({ x, y });\\n    setTargetName(\\n      element.getAttribute('aria-label') ||\\n      element.getAttribute('placeholder') ||\\n      element.textContent?.slice(0, 20) ||\\n      element.tagName.toLowerCase()\\n    );\\n    \\n    // Highlight element\\n    element.classList.add('walker-highlight');\\n    element.style.outline = `2px solid ${color}`;\\n    element.style.outlineOffset = '3px';\\n    element.style.boxShadow = `0 0 20px ${color}40`;\\n    \\n    // Remove highlight after delay\\n    setTimeout(() => {\\n      element.classList.remove('walker-highlight');\\n      element.style.outline = '';\\n      element.style.outlineOffset = '';\\n      element.style.boxShadow = '';\\n    }, speed - 100);\\n    \\n    onElementVisit?.(element, index);\\n  }, [containerRef, color, speed, onElementVisit]);\\n\\n  // Walking loop\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (!isActive || !autoStart) {\\n      setVisible(false);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n    elementsRef.current = discoverElements();\\n    \\n    if (elementsRef.current.length === 0) {\\n      setVisible(false);\\n      return;\\n    }\\n    \\n moveToElement(elementsRef.current[index], index);\\n      setCurrentIndex(index);\\n      \\n      timeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => walk(index + 1), speed);\\n    };\\n    \\n    // Start walking after small delay\\n    timeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => walk(0), 500);\\n    \\n    return () => {\\n      if (timeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(timeoutRef.current);\\n    };\\n  }, [isActive, autoStart, discoverElements, moveToElement, speed, loop, onComplete]);\\n\\n  // Cursor variants\\n  const getCursor = () => {\\n    switch (variant) {\\n      case 'hand':\\n        return <span style={{ fontSize: 28, filter: 'drop-shadow(0 2px 4px rgba(0,0,0,0.5))' }}>\\ud83d\\udc46</span>;\\n      case 'pointer':\\n        return (\\n          <svg width=\\\"24\\\" height=\\\"24\\\" viewBox=\\\"0 0 24 24\\\" fill={color}>\\n            <path d=\\\"M4 4l16 8-8 2-2 8z\\\" />\\n          </svg>\\n        );\\n      case 'dot':\\n        return (\\n          <div style={{\\n            width: 16,\\n            height: 16,\\n            borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: color,\\n            boxShadow: `0 0 20px ${color}`\\n          }} />\\n        );\\n      case 'glow':\\n        return (\\n          <div style={{\\n            width: 30,\\n            height: 30,\\n            borderRadius: '50%',\\n            background: `radial-gradient(circle, ${color} 0%, transparent 70%)`,\\n            animation: 'cursorPulse 1s infinite'\\n          }} />\\n        );\\n      default:\\n        return <span style={{ fontSize: 28 }}>\\ud83d\\udc46</span>;\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  if (!visible) return null;\\n\\n  return (\\n    <>\\n      <div\\n        style={{\\n          position: 'absolute',\\n          left: position.x,\\n          top: position.y,\\n          transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',\\n          pointerEvents: 'none',\\n          zIndex: 9999,\\n          transition: `all ${speed * 0.4}ms ease-out`\\n        }}\\n      >\\n        {getCursor()}\\n      </div>\\n      \\n      {/* Target label */}\\n      {targetName && (\\n        <div\\n          style={{\\n            position: 'absolute',\\n            left: position.x,\\n            top: position.y + 35,\\n            transform: 'translateX(-50%)',\\n            background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.8)',\\n            color: '#fff',\\n            padding: '4px 10px',\\n            borderRadius: 6,\\n            fontSize: 11,\\n            whiteSpace: 'nowrap',\\n            pointerEvents: 'none',\\n            zIndex: 9999,\\n            transition: `all ${speed * 0.3}ms opacity: 1; }\\n          50% { transform: scale(1.3); opacity: 0.7; }\\n        }\\n        .walker-highlight {\\n          transition: all 0.2s ease-out !important;\\n        }\\n      `}</style>\\n    </>\\n  );\\n};\\n\\nexport default WalkingCursor;\\nWALKINGCURSOR\\n\\necho \\\"  \\u2705 useRef<SpeechSynthesis | null>(null);\\n  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\\n\\n  // Initialize speech\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {\\n Let me guide you.\\\");\\n      setWalkerActive(false);\\n      setSelectedRole('builder');\\n    } else if (lower.includes('agent') || lower.includes('real estate') || lower.includes('realtor')) {\\n      speak(\\\"Opening agent registration. [localCompany, setLocalCompany] = useState(companyName);\n  const [localProfile, setLocalProfile] = useState(profile);\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, useState(false);\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    speak(\"Tell me about your construction business. Say your company name and what services you offer. You can also say beautify to enhance your description.\");\n    setTimeout(() => startListening(), 1000);\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (SR) {\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\n      \n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\n        let text = '';\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n        setTranscript(text);\n        \n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) {\n          setLastHeard(text);\n          processVoice(text);\n        }\n      };\n\n      recognitionRef.current.onerror = () => setIsListening(false);\n      recognitionRef.current.onend = () => { if (isListening) recognitionRef.current?.start(); };\n    }\n    return () => recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n  }, [isListening]);\n\n  const startListening = () => { try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); setIsListening(true); } catch (e) {} };\n\n  const typeIntoField = async (fieldId: string, text: string, fieldName: string, setter: (v: string) => void, parentSetter: (v: string) => void) => {\n    const el = document.getElementById(fieldId) as HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement;\n    if (!el) return;\n    \n    setFilling(fieldName);\n    el.focus();\n    el.classList.add('vv-filling');\n    \n    for (let i = 0; i <= text.length; i++) {\n      el.value = text.substring(0, i);\n      setter(text.substring(0, i));\n      await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 20));\n    }\n    \n    parentSetter(text);\n    el.classList.remove('vv-filling');\n    el.classList.add('vv-filled');\n    setTimeout(() => el.classList.remove('vv-filled'), 1000);\n    setFilling(null);\n  };\n\n  const handleBeautify = async () => {\n    if (!localProfile.trim()) {\n      speak(\"Please enter a description first.\");\n      return;\n    }\n\n    setIsBeautifying(true);\n    speak(\"Enhancing your profile description...\");\n\n    try {\n      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:1117/api/beautify', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          text: localProfile,\n          type: 'builder',\n          companyName: localCompany\n        })\n      });\n\n      const data = await response.json();\n      \n      if (data.beautified) {\n        // Typewriter effect for beautified text\n        await typeIntoField('builder-profile-textarea', data.beautified, 'Profile', setLocalProfile, onChange);\n        speak(\"Description enhanced successfully!\");\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Beautify error:', err);\n      // Fallback: Simple enhancement\n      const enhanced = `${localCompany} is a premier construction company specializing in ${localProfile}. With years of experience and a commitment to quality, we deliver exceptional results on every project.`;\n      await typeIntoField('builder-profile-textarea', enhanced, 'Profile', setLocalProfile, onChange);\n      speak(\"Description enhanced!\");\n    } finally {\n      setIsBeautifying(false);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const processVoice = useCallback(async (text: string) => {\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n    \n    // Beautify command\n    if (lower.includes('beautify') || lower.includes('enhance') || lower.includes('improve')) {\n      handleBeautify();\n      return;\n    }\n    \n    // Extract company name\n    const companyPatterns = [\n      /(?:my company is|company name is|we are|i'm from|this is)\\s+(.+?)(?:\\s+and|\\s+we|\\.|$)/i,\n      /^(.+?)\\s+(?:construction|builders|contracting|development)/i\n    ];\n    \n    for (const pattern of companyPatterns) {\n      const match = text.match(pattern);\n      if (match && match[1]) {\n        await typeIntoField('builder-company-input', match[1].trim(), 'Company Name', setLocalCompany, onCompanyChange);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Extract services/description\n    const servicePatterns = [\n      /(?:we offer|we do|we specialize in|services include|we build)\\s+(.+)/i,\n      /(?:and we|we also)\\s+(.+)/i\n    ];\n    \n    for (const pattern of servicePatterns) {\n      const match = text.match(pattern);\n      if (match && match[1]) {\n        await typeIntoField('builder-profile-textarea', match[1].trim(), 'Services', setLocalProfile, onChange);\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // Commands\n    if (lower.includes('save') || lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('continue')) {\n      if (localCompany.trim() && localProfile.trim()) onSave();\n    }\n  }, [localCompany, localProfile, onCompanyChange, onChange, onSave]);\n\n  const toggleListening = () => {\n    if (isListening) { recognitionRef.current?.stop(); setIsListening(false); }\n    else { startListening(); }\n  };\n\n  const canSave = localCompany.trim() && localProfile.trim();\n\n  return (\n    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 20 }}>\n      <div style={{ textAlign: 'center' }}>\n        <span style={{ fontSize: '2.5em' }}>\ud83c\udfd7\ufe0f</span>\n        <h3 style={{ color: THEME.accent, margin: '10px 0 5px' }}>Builder Profile</h3>\n        <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>Tell us about your construction business</p>\n      </div>\n\n      <div>\n        <label style={{ color: '#ccc', fontSize: '0.85em', display: 'block', marginBottom: 6 }}>Company Name</label>\n        <input\n          id=\"builder-company-input\"\n          type=\"text\"\n          value={localCompany}\n          onChange={e => { setLocalCompany(e.target.value); onCompanyChange(e.target.value); }}\n          placeholder=\"Your construction company name\"\n          style={{ width: '100%', padding: '14px 16px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', border: `1px solid ${THEME.accent}40`, borderRadius: 10, color: '#fff', fontSize: '1em', outline: 'none', transition: 'all 0.3s' }}\n        />\n      </div>\n\n      <div>\n        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 6 }}>\n          <label style={{ color: '#ccc', fontSize: '0.85em' }}>What construction services do you offer?</label>\n          <button\n            onClick={handleBeautify}\n            disabled={isBeautifying || !localProfile.trim()}\n            style={{\n              padding: '6px 14px',\n              borderRadius: 15,\n              border: 'none',\n              background: isBeautifying ? 'rgba(139, 92, 246, 0.3)' : 'linear-gradient(135deg, #8b5cf6, #6366f1)',\n              color: '#fff',\n              fontSize: '0.8em',\n              fontWeight: 600,\n              cursor: isBeautifying || !localProfile.trim() ? (\n              <>\u23f3 Beautifying...</>\n            ) : (\n              <>\u2728 Beautify</>\n            )}\n          </button>\n        </div>\n        <textarea\n          id=\"builder-profile-textarea\"\n          value={localProfile}\n          onChange={e => { setLocalProfile(e.target.value); onChange(e.target.value); }}\n          placeholder=\"We specialize in residential construction, renovations, custom homes...\"\n          rows={4}\n          style={{ width: '100%', padding: '14px 16px', background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', border: `1px solid ${THEME.accent}40`, borderRadius: 10, color: '#fff', fontSize: '1em', resize: 'vertical', fontFamily: 'inherit', outline: 'none', transition: 'all 0.3s' }}\n        />\n      </div>\n\n      <button onClick={onSave} disabled={!canSave} style={{ padding: '14px 40px', background: canSave ? WalkingCursor from '../common/WalkingCursor';\n\ninterface Props { onClose: () => void; onBack: () => void; }\n\ntype Step = 'phone' | 'otp' | 'preferences' | 'complete';\nconst STEPS: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'preferences', 'complete'];\nconst LABELS = ['Phone', 'Verify', 'Preferences', 'Done'];\nconst THEME = { primary: '#0f172a', secondary: '#1e293b', accent: '#06b6d4' };\n\nconst CATEGORIES = ['Flooring', 'Lighting', 'Kitchen', 'Bathroom', 'Outdoor', 'Smart Home', 'Furniture', 'Decor'];\n\nconst CustomerFlow: React.FC<Props> = ({ onClose, onBack }) => {\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState('');\n  const [selectedCategories, setSelectedCategories] = useState<string[]>([]);\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\n  const [walkerActive, setWalkerActive] = useState(true);\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\n  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\n\n  const synth = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.speechSynthesis : null;\n  const speak = useCallback((t: string) => { synth?.cancel(); const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(t); u.rate = 0.95; synth?.speak(u); }, [synth]);\n\n  const goNext = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i < STEPS.length - 1) { setStep(STEPS[i + 1]); setWalkerActive(true); } };\n  const goBack = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i > 0) setStep(STEPS[i - 1]); else onBack(); };\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const messages: Record<Step, string> = {\n      phone: \"Welcome customer! Enter your phone number to get started.\",\n      otp: \"Enter the verification code.\",\n      preferences: \"Select your interests. Say the category name to toggle.\",\n      complete: \"You're all set!\"\n    };\n    speak(messages[step]);\n    setTimeout(() => startListening(), 1000);\n  }, [step]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\n    if (SR) {\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\n        let text = '';\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\n        setTranscript(text);\n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) processVoice(text);\n      };\n      recognitionRef.current.onerror = () => setIsListening(false);\n      recognitionRef.current.onend = () => { if (isListening) recognitionRef.current?.start(); };\n    }\n    return () => recognitionRef.current?.stop();\n  }, [isListening, step, selectedCategories]);\n\n  const startListening = () => { try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); setIsListening(true); } catch (e) {} };\n  const toggleListening = () => { if (isListening) { recognitionRef.current?.stop(); setIsListening(false); } else { startListening(); } };\n\n  const processVoice = async (text: string) => {\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = { 'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0' };\n    let processed = text.toLowerCase();\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) processed = processed.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\b${word}\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\n    const digits = processed.replace(/\\D/g, '');\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\n\n    if (step === 'phone' && digits.length > 0) {\n      const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\n      setPhone(newPhone);\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) speak(\"Phone complete!\");\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'otp' && digits.length > 0) {\n      const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\n      setOtp(newOtp);\n      if (newOtp.length === 6) speak(\"Code complete!\");\n    }\n\n    if (step === 'preferences') {\n      CATEGORIES.forEach(cat => {\n        if (lower.includes(cat.toLowerCase())) {\n          setSelectedCategories(prev => {\n            if (prev.includes(cat)) {\n              speak(`Removed ${cat}`);\n              return prev.filter(c => c !== cat);\n            } else {\n              speak(`Added ${cat}`);\n              return [...prev, cat];\n            }\n          });\n        }\n      });\n    }\n\n    if (lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('continue') || lower.includes('done')) {\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) goNext();\n      else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) goNext();\n      else if (step === 'preferences') goNext();\n    }\n  };\n\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => { if (p.length <= 3) return p; if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`; return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`; };\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\n\n  const AgenticBar = () => (\n    <div style={{ marginTop: 20, padding: 16, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 16, border: `2px solid ${isListening ? STEPS: Step[] = ['phone', 'otp', 'preferences', 'complete'];\\nconst LABELS = ['Phone', 'Verify', 'Preferences', 'Done'];\\nconst THEME = { primary: '#0f172a', secondary: '#1e293b', accent: '#06b6d4' };\\n\\nconst CATEGORIES = ['Flooring', 'Lighting', 'Kitchen', 'Bathroom', 'Outdoor', 'Smart Home', 'Furniture', 'Decor'];\\n\\nconst CustomerFlow: React.FC<Props> = ({ onClose, onBack }) => {\\n  const [step, setStep] = useState<Step>('phone');\\n  const [phone, setPhone] = useState('');\\n  const [otp, setOtp] = useState('');\\n  const [selectedCategories, setSelectedCategories] = useState<string[]>([]);\\n  const [isListening, setIsListening] = useState(false);\\n  const [transcript, setTranscript] = useState('');\\n  const [walkerActive, setWalkerActive] = useState(true);\\n  const recognitionRef = useRef<any>(null);\\n  const containerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);\\n\\n  const synth = typeof window !== 'undefined' ? window.speechSynthesis : null;\\n  const speak = useCallback((t: string) => { synth?.cancel(); const u = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(t); u.rate = 0.95; synth?.speak(u); }, [synth]);\\n\\n  const goNext = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i < STEPS.length - 1) { setStep(STEPS[i + 1]); setWalkerActive(true); } };\\n  const goBack = () => { const i = STEPS.indexOf(step); if (i > 0) setStep(STEPS[i - 1]); else onBack(); };\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const messages: Record<Step, string> = {\\n      phone: \\\"Welcome customer! Enter your phone number to get started.\\\",\\n      otp: \\\"Enter the verification code.\\\",\\n      preferences: \\\"Select your interests. Say the category name to toggle.\\\",\\n      complete: \\\"You're all set!\\\"\\n    };\\n    speak(messages[step]);\\n    setTimeout(() => startListening(), 1000);\\n  }, [step]);\\n\\n  useEffect(() => {\\n    const SR = (window as any).SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition;\\n    if (SR) {\\n      recognitionRef.current = new SR();\\n      recognitionRef.current.continuous = true;\\n      recognitionRef.current.interimResults = true;\\n      recognitionRef.current.onresult = (event: any) => {\\n        let text = '';\\n        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) text += event.results[i][0].transcript;\\n        setTranscript(text);\\n        if (event.results[event.resultIndex].isFinal) processVoice(text);\\n      };\\n      recognitionRef.current.onerror = () => setIsListening(false);\\n      recognitionRef.current.onend = () => { if (isListening) recognitionRef.current?.start(); };\\n    }\\n    return () => recognitionRef.current?.stop();\\n  }, [isListening, step, selectedCategories]);\\n\\n  const startListening = () => { try { recognitionRef.current?.start(); setIsListening(true); } catch (e) {} };\\n  const toggleListening = () => { if (isListening) { recognitionRef.current?.stop(); setIsListening(false); } else { startListening(); } };\\n\\n  const processVoice = async (text: string) => {\\n    const numberWords: Record<string, string> = { 'zero': '0', 'one': '1', 'two': '2', 'three': '3', 'four': '4', 'five': '5', 'six': '6', 'seven': '7', 'eight': '8', 'nine': '9', 'oh': '0' };\\n    let processed = text.toLowerCase();\\n    for (const [word, digit] of Object.entries(numberWords)) processed = processed.replace(new RegExp(`\\\\\\\\b${word}\\\\\\\\b`, 'g'), digit);\\n    const digits = processed.replace(/\\\\D/g, '');\\n    const lower = text.toLowerCase();\\n\\n    if (step === 'phone' && digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newPhone = (phone + digits).slice(0, 10);\\n      setPhone(newPhone);\\n      if (newPhone.length === 10) speak(\\\"Phone complete!\\\");\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'otp' && digits.length > 0) {\\n      const newOtp = (otp + digits).slice(0, 6);\\n      setOtp(newOtp);\\n      if (newOtp.length === 6) speak(\\\"Code complete!\\\");\\n    }\\n\\n    if (step === 'preferences') {\\n      CATEGORIES.forEach(cat => {\\n        if (lower.includes(cat.toLowerCase())) {\\n          setSelectedCategories(prev => {\\n            if (prev.includes(cat)) {\\n              speak(`Removed ${cat}`);\\n              return prev.filter(c => c !== cat);\\n            } else {\\n              speak(`Added ${cat}`);\\n              return [...prev, cat];\\n            }\\n          });\\n        }\\n      });\\n    }\\n\\n    if (lower.includes('next') || lower.includes('continue') || lower.includes('done')) {\\n      if (step === 'phone' && phone.length === 10) goNext();\\n      else if (step === 'otp' && otp.length === 6) goNext();\\n      else if (step === 'preferences') goNext();\\n    }\\n  };\\n\\n  const formatPhone = (p: string) => { if (p.length <= 3) return p; if (p.length <= 6) return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3)}`; return `${p.slice(0,3)}-${p.slice(3,6)}-${p.slice(6)}`; };\\n  const stepIndex = STEPS.indexOf(step);\\n\\n  const AgenticBar = () => (\\n    <div style={{ marginTop: 20, padding: 16, background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 16, border: `2px solid ${isListening ? '#10b981' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.1)'}` }}>\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10, marginBottom: 12 }}>\\n        <div style={{ width: 10, height: 10, borderRadius: '50%', background: isListening ? '#10b981' : '#64748b', animation: isListening ? 'pulse 1s infinite' : 'none' }} />\\n        <span style={{ color: '#06b6d4', fontSize: '0.9em' }}>\\ud83c\\udfa4 {isListening ? 'LISTENING' : 'READY'}</span>\\n      </div>\\n      {isListening && (<div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 3, height: 25, alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 10 }}>{[...Array(12)].map((_, i) => (<div key={i} style={{ width: 3, background: 'linear-gradient(to top, #10b981, #06b6d4)', borderRadius: 2, animation: `wave 0.4s ease-in-out ${i * 0.05}s infinite alternate`, height: 8 }} />))}</div>)}\\n      {transcript && (<div style={{ background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.3)', borderRadius: 8, padding: '10px 14px', marginBottom: 12 }}><p style={{ color: '#e2e8f0', margin: 0 }}>\\\"{transcript}\\\"</p></div>)}\\n      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 10 }}>\\n        <button onClick={toggleListening} style={{ padding: '10px 24px', borderRadius: 25, border: 'none', background: isListening ? '#ef4444' : '#10b981', color: 'white', fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer' }}>{isListening ?
